< Text>
Had a great experience here today; I was a bit nervous before going, after reading some of the reviews, but didn't have much choice as nothing nearby was open on the weekends.

I had a flat tire, and called ahead to ask if I could have my car towed there--the woman on the phone was very helpful and friendly and said to bring it on over, and that they actually have my size tire in stock. In the past at other shops I've had to wait several days because my tire needed to be ordered (Smart car), so that was a nice surprise.

When I got there she was up-front about costs and honest about how long it'd take. I walked home thinking I probably wouldn't have my car back today, but 2 hours later she called to tell me it was ready! Very happy customer, and I'd definitely go back again if necessary.<//Text>

<Text>I took over a lease at Copper Beech and lived in the apartment for 2.5 months and paid a total of $1,500 in rent. During my time there, I was rarely in the apartment, never wore shoes inside, never had any guests, and kept things clean and tidy. Upon moving out, I spent about 5-6 hours cleaning and left the place in pristine condition. Copper Beech then charged me $264.66 for general cleaning, carpet cleaning, and painting! Do the math and $264.66 divided by $1,500 comes out to paying 17.6% more than I agreed to pay in rent.

When I tried to voice this concern in person, I was told that the property manager Melanie doesn't take appointments. I sent an email and got a response 14 days later (even though it said in writing that it would take no more than 3 days) saying these charges were just "part of the process [...] of getting the unit ready for the next resident".

Does this sound fair to you?

I have rented in four other places before this and never had any issues. Fresno is a large town and I recommend looking on craigslist or roomies.com for other options that are cheaper and have a sense of honesty. This is my first Google review because I get peeved when individuals are grotesquely unfair.< /Text>< Gmap_id>

The reviews on this site are negative, but let me give you some other perspective on what they wrote.  The apartment that was open for tours was mine.  The management paid us to show our apartment on the condition that we kept it clean.  I ended up in the hospital, and we had a difficult time on a couple of occasions.  The management would always announce coming tours.  They never showed up unannounced (even if we were not home). Management does not show random apartments.

As for the roaches, I admit that there were roaches in the garage, but they were always dead. I mostly see them by the garbage, but I haven't seen any since seeing a new exterminator.

My family moved into Copper Beech last August of 2012 and we couldn't be happier. We love the spaciousness of the townhome and with 3 boys and a family of 5 we feel like we have plenty of space. Anytime we have had a concern or maintenance issue it has been addressed quickly and efficiently. The staff treats us with respect and is extremely professional. We enjoy all of the special events and contests they hold here. There are always opportunities to receive special perks and prizes. They go out of there way to show there appreciation for their tenants. Even though our lease isn't up until August we had NO hesitation in deciding to stay another year. We are looking forward to the pool opening soon which was ALWAYS clean and inviting. Our decision to move here has made all 5 of us happy and we feel like we have a wonderful "home" not just an apartment to live in.</Review>

< text>
Great experience for my first visit.   Flavorful and inexpensive Mexican lunch buffet.  It's even cheaper than El Torito.  The food quality is good and tasty.  Options are limited but enough for you to choose from, and it will fill you up.  I came for their weekday lunch buffet 11am-2pm for $11.99.  Drinks are not included on the price.  Buffet includes menudo, caldo de albondigas, chile rellenos, rolled taquitos, chicken fajita, enchiladas, rice and beans, chile verde con carne, pork carnitas, salsa, pico de gallo, and much more.  Service staff are very helpful and friendly.  Plenty of parking.  I will definitely come back again.<//text>

<text>Great place to eat with more than one location.  Not generic food.  Great food that's a cross between Mexican and Cuban. Large portions at very reasonable prices--  actually lower than expected.  Excellent staff.  They will even make things that aren't on the menu, so don't be afraid to ask.  I always get the Carne Asada plate with an order of fried platanos ( bananas).  They'll fry them plain, or add cinnamon and sugar.  They are wonderful either way and its always enough that I can take home leftovers for a complete meal the next day!!   They have a special lunch menu and a lunch Buffett. So far haven't come across anything that I wouldn't order or recommend.  Best Mexican restraunt in southern California, in my opinion.< /text>< Rating>

Today, my mood led me toward Margaritaville (maybe hearing it on the radio
had something to do with it...do you think?)

Damn subliminal messaging worked again!
Anyways, I sat at the bar and said to the bartender "I need a damn good tasting Margarita like I'm use to...he smiled and said that he can make it happen.

He brought me my Margarita and said to taste it because I came in at a good time.
After sipping it twice (I wanted to make sure before I spoke.)
I told him that it was a damn good tasting Margarita and will enjoy the rest once I decide on what to eat.

It was at this time, that he handed me a small bar menu which had several different "Happy Hour" food selections that all looked delicious.

After deciding on the Burrito with the chunks of pork which was marinated with a green sauce inside. I asked if it we're possible to make it "Wet with the red enchilada sauce"
He said no problem because it automatically is served that way.

Circling back to when he mentioned about coming in at a good time, he told me the wet burrito was $7.00 and the Margarita is only $4.00..such a deal.

I responded with a smile and said "that is incredible and let's get this show on the road.
It was about 10 min.that passed and he was already bringing out this large wet size burrito (with ez on the melting cheese.)

Let me tell you, that I enjoyed every last bite as I slathered some sour cream on top. I took a breather for about 5 min. and then finished off the second half with equal enjoyment.
I want to thank the bartender who worked the early afternoon shift for making my visit an enjoyable one. As usual, I'll be back.

<Date>1489188480791< /Date>< text>
Changed my rating from 2 to 4 stars.. We returned to Casa Gaming yesterday even though I had previously said I wasn't going to return.  This visit I gotta admit the food was very tasty. I ordered a soft Carnitas taco, enchilada on the dinner menu (there menu is extensive). My meal was very good. They serve chips before we ordered; the chips were thin, warm and the taste is excellent. The salsa is good; I add Pica de Gallo to add flavor to chips and my meal.

Before this recent visit I said:

The food was okay (about 3 stars). The interior is also 3 stars, exterior 2 stars.

Big problem with this restaurant (my visit) though, the margarita was terrible. Even worse than the terrible margarita was when I mentioned it to the manager he did nothing to make me a happy customer, not even offer to take it off my check. That reflects very poor management and showing me that he evidently doesn't care if I return. I had taken a small drink and asked the person I was with to taste it also. I asked him to look at the margarita, taste it, but he wouldn't do either. Both of us (his customers) agree it was very bad.

I was a bit persistent with the manager just how bad it was.."the worst margarita I have ever had", I told him. The waiter when asked about the drink told the manager with a shrug that it was a "Happy Hour" margarita...does that mean they serve bad margaritas during Happy Hour?

A side note on this is that one member of the family does like this restaurant and dines there fairly regularly; it reminds her of her family outings (but she drinks wine not the margaritas). She had warned me that the margaritas were bad.. I am sorry I didn't listen to her. I mean, how can you mess up a margarita? She said, "I love there food but I order a glass of wine, they can't ruin that).

In one other visit, I did like the Buffet.

I am not returning. Also, I can't recommend this restaurant with poor management because poor management is unacceptable.

cmilton111</text>
